#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有自动驾驶系统通常在有限地理区域内训练和评估，部署到新城市时因外观、道路拓扑和交通模式的显著域偏移导致性能严重下降，而基于域适应、数据增强或合成数据生成的方法依赖目标域标注、城市特定标注或任务特定设计，可扩展性和有效性受限。

**Method:** 本文提出了CityGen，一个基于扩散模型的生成框架，通过高清地图条件合成和城市级视觉提示引导，实现零标签的城市适应，并构建了CityTransfer-Bench，一个地理不相交的跨城市泛化基准，用于评估感知、分割和规划任务的跨城市泛化能力。

**Result:** 大量实验表明，CityGen在感知、分割和规划等多个任务上一致地提升了跨城市鲁棒性，证明了其作为可扩展且标签高效的泛化基础的有效性。

**Conclusion:** CityGen为通用自动驾驶建立了一个可扩展且标签高效的泛化基础，无需目标域标签即可有效提升跨城市部署的鲁棒性，有望推动自动驾驶系统在新城市中的快速部署。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Autonomous driving systems are commonly trained and evaluated within limited geographic regions, which hinders their scalability when deployed in new cities. However, significant domain shifts in appearance, road topology, and traffic patterns often cause severe performance degradation under cross-city deployment. Existing approaches based on domain adaptation, data augmentation, or synthetic data generation typically rely on labeled target data, city-specific annotations, or task-specific designs, limiting their scalability and effectiveness for holistic evaluation. In this paper, we introduce CityTransfer-Bench, a geographically disjoint benchmark for evaluating cross-city generalization across perception, segmentation, and planning, and propose CityGen, a diffusion-based generative framework that performs zero-label city adaptation via HD-map-conditioned synthesis guided by city-level visual prompts. Extensive experiments demonstrate that CityGen consistently improves cross-city robustness across multiple tasks, establishing a scalable and label-efficient foundation for generalizable autonomous driving.


### [32] [EVL-ECG: Efficient ECG Interpretation With Multi-Aspect Heterogeneous Knowledge Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29977)
*Dang Hong Nguyen, Nhi Ngoc-Yen Nguyen, Huy-Hieu Pham*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
EVL-ECG 提出了一种面向心电信号跨架构知识蒸馏框架，通过多头交叉注意力对齐、最优传输视觉特征匹配和几何内架构关系匹配三项技术，在保持诊断逻辑的前提下实现高效模型压缩，在基准上提升 2.4% AUC 和 1.1% 临床准确率，并构建了适合资源受限临床环境的 2B 参数心电基础模型。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 高保真心电信号解读日益依赖大规模基础模型，但其极端计算需求阻碍了在临床边缘设备上的部署；传统知识蒸馏方法在处理异构架构间的时空依赖关系时效果不佳，无法有效迁移心电信号的复杂时空特征与诊断逻辑。

**Method:** EVL-ECG 提出三项核心创新：多头交叉注意力对齐用于协调异构架构差异以保留细粒度形态学特征；基于最优传输的视觉特征匹配用于在 token 表示不匹配的情况下保持各导联间的全局结构关系；几何内架构关系匹配用于蒸馏教师模型潜在的诊断推理逻辑，从而实现跨架构的心电诊断逻辑高效蒸馏。

**Result:** 在多个心电基准上，EVL-ECG 相较于现有基线方法实现了 2.4% AUC 提升和 1.1% 临床准确率提升，并成功构建了一个仅 2B 参数的高效心电基础模型，适用于资源受限的临床环境。

**Conclusion:** EVL-ECG 通过面向心电信号的跨架构知识蒸馏方法，有效解决了大规模基础模型在临床边缘部署中的计算瓶颈，验证了保留诊断逻辑的结构化知识迁移对模型压缩的重要性，为心电信号分析的实用化部署提供了可行路径。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
High-fidelity ECG interpretation is increasingly reliant on massive foundation models, yet their deployment in clinical edge-care remains hindered by extreme computational demands. While knowledge distillation (KD) is a promising solution, traditional methods fail to capture the complex spatio-temporal dependencies of ECG signals when transferring knowledge across heterogeneous architectures. In this paper, we propose EVL-ECG, a framework specifically designed for cross-architecture distillation of cardiac diagnostic logic. EVL-ECG introduces three ECG-aware innovations: (1) Multi-Head Cross-Attention Alignment, which harmonizes architectural discrepancies to preserve fine-grained morphological features; (2) Optimal Transport-based Visual Feature Matching, utilizing optimal transport to maintain global structural relationships across ECG leads despite mismatched token representations; and (3) Geometric Intra-Architecture Relation Matching, which distills the latent diagnostic reasoning of the teacher model. Evaluations across ECG benchmarks demonstrate that EVL-ECG yields improvements of up to 2.4% AUC and 1.1% clinical accuracy over existing baselines. Notably, EVL-ECG establishes an efficient 2B-parameter ECG foundation model, suitable for resource-constrained clinical environments.


### [33] [FRUC: Feedforward Dynamic Scene Reconstruction from Uncalibrated Collaborative Driving Views](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29997)
*Yihang Tao, Yu Guo, Zhengru Fang, Haonan An, Yuguang Fang*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
FRUC提出了一种基于前馈3D高斯泼溅的框架，用于从无标定的协作驾驶视角进行动态场景重建，通过引入以自我为中心的因果遮挡场和零初始化残差去噪过程，实现了一次性、免标定的跨智能体协作盲点补全，在渲染质量和效率上均达到新SOTA。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有面向多智能体协同驾驶场景的重建方法存在两大瓶颈：一是依赖精确的空间标定（如相机外参对齐），二是在每个场景上都需要耗时的逐场景优化，无法满足实时或在线协作重建的需求。此外，在无标定条件下进行跨智能体信息融合时，如何不破坏自车已准确观测的可见几何，同时增强被遮挡区域的几何信息，仍是一个未被充分解决的问题。

**Method:** FRUC以视觉引导的几何Transformer骨干网络为基础，实现了从灵活数量的多车辆视角中进行一次推理、免标定的3D高斯泼溅重建。该方法首先引入一个以自我为中心的因果遮挡场，通过建模智能体间的时空相关性，显式地推导出遮挡演化作为潜在先验；然后在这些遮挡先验的引导下，将跨智能体信息融合形式化为一个确定性的残差去噪过程，通过零初始化注入将具有挑战性的跨智能体融合转化为有界残差学习，从而实现鲁棒的协作盲点补全。

**Result:** 在真实世界数据集V2XReal和UrbanIng-V2X上的大量实验表明，FRUC在动态协作驾驶场景的场景重建任务上达到了新SOTA水平，在渲染质量和效率两方面均显著优于现有方法。

**Conclusion:** FRUC通过将分布式多车辆网络概念化为时空非结构化的以自我为中心的多相机系统，为无标定协作感知场景重建提供了高效可行的方案，其非破坏性几何补充策略有望推动协作自动驾驶中实时在线重建的实际部署。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
We present FRUC, a feed-forward 3D Gaussian splatting framework for dynamic scene reconstruction from uncalibrated collaborative driving views. Existing multi-agent reconstruction frameworks are often hindered by rigid prerequisites, demanding precise spatial calibration and slow per-scene optimization. In this paper, we rethink this task by conceptualizing a distributed multi-vehicle network as a spatio-temporally unstructured ego-centric multi-camera system, where the core challenge lies in enhancing ego-centric occluded geometry through collaboration without degrading the ego's accurately observed visible geometry, while preserving reconstruction efficiency. For efficient reconstruction, FRUC is built upon a visual grounded geometric Transformer backbone to enable one-shot, calibration-free inference from a flexible number of multi-vehicle views. To achieve non-destructive geometric supplementation under uncalibrated cross-agent misalignment, FRUC first introduces an ego-centric causal occlusion field that explicitly derives occlusion evolution as latent priors by modeling agent-wise spatio-temporal correlations. Guided by these occlusion priors, it further formulates cross-agent integration as a deterministic residual denoising process via zero-initialized injection, turning challenging cross-agent fusion into bounded residual learning for robust collaborative blind-spot completion. Through extensive evaluations on the real-world V2XReal and UrbanIng-V2X datasets, FRUC is shown to be a new state-of-the-art for the scene reconstruction of dynamic collaborative driving environments, significantly outperforming existing methods in both rendering quality and efficiency.


### [34] [FakeVLM-R1: Internalizing Physical Laws via CoT for Synthetic Image Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30062)
*Leqi Zhu, Junyan Ye, Kaiqing Lin, Zhiyuan Yan, Conghui He, Weijia Li*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
FakeVLM-R1 提出结合 GRPO 与批判性思维链（Critical Thinking CoT）的框架，在监督微调基础上赋予大多模态模型因果推理能力，实现高精度、可解释的合成图像检测，并在多个基准上取得 SOTA 性能，同时解决了现有方法对真实图像的过度拒绝偏差问题。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有基于大多模态模型的合成图像可解释检测方法依赖海量伪造数据的模仿学习，缺乏真正的因果推理能力，容易产生解释性幻觉；同时存在对真实图像的过度拒绝偏差，亟需一种具备人类级批判性思维能力的检测框架。

**Method:** FakeVLM-R1 在监督微调（SFT）基础上，引入组相对策略优化（GRPO）与批判性思维链（Critical Thinking CoT）机制。推理阶段执行“双向辩证推理”：提出伪造假设的同时调用物理常识构建真实性反证。此外构建了 FakeClue++ 数据集，引入基于真实图像物理规律的注释作为统一真实性锚点。

**Result:** FakeVLM-R1 在多个基准上达到 SOTA 性能，实现了高精度且逻辑可解释的检测，解决了现有方法对真实图像的过度拒绝偏差，并展现出良好的泛化性与抗扰动鲁棒性。

**Conclusion:** 通过强化学习与因果推理机制的结合，FakeVLM-R1 有效克服了基于模仿学习的解释性幻觉问题，为合成图像检测提供了一种兼具高精度与可解释性的新范式，其泛化与鲁棒性优势表明了该方法在实际应用中的潜力。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
The development of generative artificial intelligence technologies has propelled the visual realism of synthetic images to an unprecedented level. Although current interpretable detection methods based on Large Multimodal Models (LMMs) have made certain progress, they still rely on imitation learning derived from massive volumes of forged data. Consequently, they lack genuine causal reasoning capabilities and are prone to explanatory hallucinations. To overcome this bottleneck, we propose FakeVLM-R1, aiming to endow the model with human-like critical thinking capabilities when performing synthetic detection tasks. Building upon Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT), this framework integrates Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) with a Critical Thinking Chain-of-Thought (CoT) mechanism. During the inference phase, the model executes a "bidirectional dialectical reasoning" process: while proposing a forgery hypothesis, it must simultaneously invoke physical commonsense to construct an authenticity counter-proof. Furthermore, we constructed the FakeClue++ dataset with high-quality samples, which extensively introduces annotations guided by the physical laws of authentic images, providing a unified authenticity anchor for the model. Experiments confirm that FakeVLM-R1 achieves SOTA performance the evaluated models across multiple benchmarks. It not only achieves high-precision, logically interpretable detection but also resolves the over-rejection bias of existing methods against real images, demonstrating generalization and robustness against perturbations.


### [35] [Geometry Matters: 3D Foundation Priors for Learning Semantic Correspondence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30093)
*Artur Jesslen, Olaf Dünkel, Adam Kortylewski*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
提出一种3D感知的后训练框架，利用SAM3D等3D基础模型生成几何感知特征图，并结合DINO和Stable Diffusion特征以及测地距离过滤，训练轻量级适配器，在无需姿态标注的情况下提升语义对应估计的3D感知能力。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有的自监督视觉模型和文本到图像扩散模型的基础特征主要从2D图像目标中学习，缺乏显式的3D感知，因此容易混淆对称物体侧面、重复部件以及在3D中不同但视觉上相似的结构，导致语义对应估计不准确。

**Method:** 提出一个3D感知后训练框架，利用SAM3D估计物体几何和姿态，并通过渲染-比较优化精炼姿态；随后从重建几何中渲染PartField描述符到图像平面，生成几何感知特征图以补充DINO和Stable Diffusion特征；利用重建形状上的测地距离过滤候选对应点，将过滤后的匹配作为监督信号训练DINO和Stable Diffusion之上的轻量级适配器，用于语义对应估计。

**Result:** 实验表明，该方法的语义对应估计性能优于现有方法，同时减少了对人工几何监督的依赖；相比依赖姿态标注和粗略球面几何的先前后训练方法，本方法自动获取实例特定的3D结构并指导对应学习。

**Conclusion:** 通过引入3D基础模型先验，可以在无需姿态标注的情况下有效提升2D基础特征的3D感知能力，为语义对应估计提供了一种更高效且几何更准确的训练范式。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Foundation features from self-supervised vision models and text-to-image diffusion models have proven effective for semantic correspondence estimation. However, because these features are learned primarily from 2D image objectives, they lack explicit 3D awareness and often confuse symmetric object sides, repeated parts, and visually similar structures that are distinct in 3D. We introduce a 3D-aware post-training framework that goes beyond available 2D foundation features by incorporating priors from 3D foundation models. Given an image, our method uses SAM3D to estimate object geometry and pose, and refines the pose through render-and-compare optimization. Subsequently, we render PartField descriptors from the reconstructed geometry into the image plane based on the estimated object pose. The resulting geometry-aware feature maps complement DINO and Stable Diffusion features, while geodesic distances on the reconstructed shapes enable reliable filtering of candidate correspondences. We use the filtered matches as supervision to train a lightweight adapter on top of DINO and Stable Diffusion for semantic correspondence. In contrast to prior post-training approaches that require pose annotations and rely on coarse spherical geometry, our method automatically obtains instance-specific 3D structure and uses it to guide correspondence learning. Experiments show that our approach improves semantic correspondence over the prior methods while reducing manual geometric supervision. Code and model can be found at https:/github.com/GenIntel/3D-SC.


### [36] [xModel-KD: Cross-modal Knowledge Distillation for 3D Scene Perception using LiDAR](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30111)
*Thenukan Pathmanathan, Kanchan Keisham, Thangarajah Akilan*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
提出跨模态知识蒸馏框架xModel-KD，通过2D图像纹理与3D点云几何的对齐学习统一逐点表征，在无需大规模密集标注的条件下提升点云分割性能，在mIoU上相比纯LiDAR基线提升2%。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 点云分割受限于3D密集标注的高成本与稀缺性，同时单一模态存在固有缺陷：2D图像缺乏深度与几何结构，3D点云稀疏且无纹理信息。现有跨模态方法多依赖大规模标注数据集且未充分用于数据高效的密集预测任务，亟需一种能利用多模态互补优势且无需大量标注的解决方案。

**Method:** 提出xModel-KD跨模态知识蒸馏框架，核心包括一个跨模态融合编码器，通过对比学习目标在多个视图下强制对应的2D与3D表征之间的特征一致性。该方法整合了强大的预训练骨干网络与定向融合策略，将2D图像的外观线索有效迁移至几何感知的点云特征中，实现跨模态对齐下的统一逐点表征学习。

**Result:** 实验结果表明，所提出的跨模态融合方法在点云分割任务上相比纯LiDAR基线实现了2%的mIoU绝对提升，验证了利用互补多模态信息在可扩展且标注高效的3D场景理解中的有效性。

**Conclusion:** 通过知识蒸馏实现2D纹理与3D几何的跨模态对齐，能够在不依赖大规模密集标注的情况下显著提升点云分割性能，为数据高效的3D场景理解提供了可行路径，表明多模态互补信息的有效融合是缓解标注稀缺问题的重要手段。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Point cloud segmentation is a fundamental task in 3D scene understanding. Its progress is constrained by the high cost and time required for dense 3D annotations, making labeled samples difficult to obtain. Beyond annotation scarcity, different sensing modalities face inherent limitations. 2D images provide rich texture and appearance cues, yet they lack explicit depth and geometric structure. In contrast, 3D point clouds capture accurate spatial geometry but are sparse and contain no texture information. As a result, relying on a single modality restricts the richness of learned representations and weakens generalization. Although recent multi-modal methods that combine 3D point clouds with 2D images have demonstrated strong performance in tasks such as classification and retrieval, they typically depend on large-scale labeled datasets and have not been fully exploited for data-efficient dense prediction. To address these limitations, we propose a novel cross-modal knowledge distillation framework, xModel-KD, for 3D point cloud segmentation. Our method exploits the complementary strengths of 2D texture and 3D geometry by learning unified per-point representations through cross-modal alignment. Specifically, we design a cross-modal fusion encoder trained with a contrastive objective that enforces feature consistency between corresponding 2D and 3D representations across multiple views. By integrating powerful pre-trained backbones with a targeted fusion strategy, the proposed framework effectively transfers appearance cues from images to geometry-aware point features. Experimental results show that cross-modal fusion achieves a 2% absolute improvement in mIoU over a LiDAR-only baseline, demonstrating the benefit of leveraging complementary multi-modal information for scalable and annotation-efficient 3D scene understanding.


### [37] [PARCEL: Pool-Anchored Resampling with Conditioned Elastic Queries for Efficient Vision-Language Understanding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30126)
*Selim Kuzucu, Alessio Tonioni, Vasile Lup, Bernt Schiele, Federico Tombari, Muhammad Ferjad Naeem*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
PARCEL提出了一种池锚定弹性查询视觉分词架构，通过将空间池令牌作为低频布局锚点并基于池条件查询重采样引导弹性查询令牌关注互补视觉特征，解决了现有弹性视觉压缩方法在激进压缩下因空间压缩混叠和查询压缩丢失空间定位导致性能下降的问题，在27个基准测试中持续超越现有弹性基线。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 大型视觉语言模型将视觉输入映射为密集令牌序列，导致推理时二次计算瓶颈。现有弹性视觉令牌压缩方法（如嵌套池化、嵌套查询重采样）在激进压缩下表现不佳：空间压缩类方法相当于不完美的低通滤波器，引发频谱混叠模糊细节；查询压缩类方法用非局部摘要替代网格对齐令牌，严重损害空间定位能力。现有方法在高效保留细粒度视觉信息和空间定位能力之间存在表征冲突。

**Method:** PARCEL提出池锚定重采样与条件弹性查询架构（Pool-Anchored Resampling with Conditioned Elastic Queries），核心思想是将特征提取任务动态分工：将空间池令牌（spatial pool tokens）设为低频布局锚点，通过池条件查询重采样（Pool-Conditioned Query Resampling）使弹性查询令牌（elastic query tokens）以这些锚点为条件，从而引导查询令牌关注互补的视觉特征而非冗余的空间映射。该方法支持单一模型在多个视觉令牌预算下运行，保持"一次训练、随处部署"的范式。

**Result:** 在27个基准测试上的广泛评估表明，PARCEL能有效改进性能-效率帕累托前沿，在不同视觉令牌预算下持续优于现有嵌套（matryoshka）基线方法，同时保留了无需重新训练即可在不同压缩率下部署的弹性特性。

**Conclusion:** PARCEL通过有效的空间-查询分工机制解决了弹性视觉压缩中空间细节保留与空间定位能力之间的冲突，证明了分离低频结构锚点与弹性查询表征的设计原则在视觉语言模型高效推理中的有效性，为弹性视觉分词架构提供了新的设计方向。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Large Vision-Language Models (LVLMs) map visual inputs into dense token sequences, imposing a quadratic computational bottleneck for inference. Elastic visual-token compression addresses this by training a single model that can run at multiple visual-token budgets. However, existing approaches struggle under aggressive compression. Spatial-only compression, as in nested pooling, behaves as an imperfect low-pass filter and induces spectral aliasing that obscures fine-grained detail. Query-only compression, as in nested query resampling, replaces explicit grid-aligned tokens with non-local summaries and substantially degrades spatial grounding. To resolve this representational conflict, we introduce PARCEL (Pool-Anchored Resampling with Conditioned Elastic Queries for Efficient Vision-Language Understanding), a visual tokenization architecture that dynamically partitions the labor of feature extraction. PARCEL establishes spatial pool tokens as low-frequency layout anchors and conditions elastic query tokens on these anchors through Pool-Conditioned Query Resampling. This encourages query tokens to focus on complementary visual features rather than redundant spatial mapping. Extensive evaluations across 27 benchmarks show that PARCEL improves the performance-efficiency Pareto frontier, consistently outperforming existing matryoshka baselines across visual-token budgets while preserving the "train once, deploy anywhere" paradigm.


### [38] [AnomalyAgent: Training-Free Agentic Models for Zero-/Few-Shot Anomaly Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30140)
*Yi Zhang, Jiawen Zhu, Lele Fu, Guansong Pang*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
AnomalyAgent是一个无需训练、基于智能体框架的异常检测方法，利用多模态大语言模型的推理能力，在零样本和少样本设置下显著优于现有基于VLM的异常检测方法，能够检测简单表面缺陷和复杂的逻辑/上下文异常。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有基于CLIP等视觉-语言模型的零样本/少样本异常检测方法虽然泛化性好，但需要大量辅助数据集进行训练才能将VLM适配到异常检测任务，且其依赖视觉-文本嵌入相似度的异常评分缺乏推理能力，无法检测需要深度上下文理解的复杂异常（如逻辑/上下文异常）。

**Method:** AnomalyAgent提出了一种无需训练的智能体框架，核心包含两个关键组件：1）一套全面的异常中心工具集，使多模态大语言模型能够在零样本设置下进行自适应、智能体驱动的异常推理；2）一个定制化的记忆模块，通过少样本上下文参考示例来支撑异常推理。

**Result:** 在包含简单表面缺陷（如裂纹、凹痕和明显病变）的传统基准以及物流和制造场景中的逻辑/上下文异常等更多样化异常类型上的实验表明，AnomalyAgent在零样本和少样本异常检测设置下，其性能显著优于无需训练的VLM异常检测方法和通用智能体方法，展现出优越的泛化能力。

**Conclusion:** AnomalyAgent证明了利用多模态大语言模型的推理和泛化能力可以在无需额外训练的情况下有效解决异常检测任务，尤其是在需要深度上下文理解的复杂异常场景中，为训练自由的智能体驱动异常检测提供了新范式。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Benefiting from generalizability of vision-language models (VLMs) such as CLIP, many zero-/few-shot anomaly detection (AD) approaches have achieved impressive detection performance across various datasets. Nevertheless, they require substantial training on large auxiliary datasets to adapt VLMs to anomaly detection, and their inference largely relies on visual-text embedding similarity-based anomaly scores, lacking reasoning abilities to detect complex anomalies that require in-depth contextual understanding. To address this limitation, we propose \textbf{AnomalyAgent}, a novel training-free, agentic framework that leverages the advanced reasoning and generalization capabilities of multimodal large language models (MLLMs) for anomaly detection. The key ingredients include \textbf{1)} a comprehensive anomaly-centric toolset that enables adaptive MLLM-driven, agentic anomaly reasoning in zero-shot settings, and \textbf{2)} a customized memory module that grounds anomaly reasoning with few-shot, in-context reference examples. We extend evaluation beyond the detection of simple anomalies (e.g., surface defects like cracks and dents and clear lesions) in widely used benchmarks to more diverse types of anomalies such as logical/contextual anomalies in logistics and manufacturing settings. Extensive experiment results demonstrate that our AnomalyAgent achieves substantially better performance compared to training-free VLM-based AD and generic agentic methods, highlighting its superior generalization capability in both zero-shot and few-shot anomaly detection settings. The code implementation can be find at this address.


### [39] [Why Far Looks Up: Probing Spatial Representation in Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30161)
*Cheolhong Min, Jaeyun Jung, Daeun Lee, Hyeonseong Jeon, Yu Su, Jonathan Tremblay, Chan Hee Song, Jaesik Park*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文提出了一种表征级分析框架，揭示了视觉语言模型在空间推理中普遍存在"垂直-距离纠缠"偏差——将图像中垂直位置与距离错误关联，该偏差随数据规模扩大而加剧且与模型族无关，并构建了合成基准SpatialTunnel以隔离和度量该偏差。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 尽管视觉语言模型在空间推理基准上表现优异，但其是否真正具备结构化的3D空间理解能力，抑或仅仅依赖自然图像中的统计捷径仍不明确；现有评估方法无法从表征层面诊断模型内部空间轴的组织方式与解耦程度。

**Method:** 提出一个表征级分析框架，通过构建最小对比对来测量VLM嵌入中空间轴的组织与解耦程度；引入合成基准SpatialTunnel，通过去除自然图像中的常见相关性来暴露空间捷径偏差。

**Result:** 跨多个模型族的分析一致揭示了"垂直-距离纠缠"偏差：模型将图像中的垂直位置与距离混淆，模仿了自然照片的透视偏差；该偏差导致视角一致样本与反启发式样本之间存在显著准确率差距，并随数据规模扩大而加剧；具有相似基准分数的模型在内部表征上存在差异，且这些差异可预测跨不同空间推理基准的准确率与鲁棒性；SpatialTunnel实验确认该纠缠是模型内在的，空间轴分离良好的模型表现出更强的鲁棒性。

**Conclusion:** 垂直-距离纠缠是视觉语言模型中与模型族无关的内在偏差，数据规模扩大会强化而非缓解该偏差；良好的空间表征结构（空间轴良好分离）是实现鲁棒空间推理的关键，模型内部表征的差异可作为跨基准性能的预测指标。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Vision-language models (VLMs) achieve strong performance on spatial reasoning benchmarks, yet it remains unclear whether this reflects structured 3D understanding or reliance on statistical shortcuts in natural images. We introduce a representation-level analysis framework that constructs minimal contrastive pairs to measure how spatial axes are organized and disentangled within VLM embeddings. Our analysis across multiple model families reveals a consistent vertical-distance entanglement: models conflate vertical image position with distance, mirroring the perspective bias of natural photographs. This bias produces a significant accuracy gap between perspective-consistent and counter-heuristic examples, and intensifies under data scaling even as overall benchmark accuracy improves. We further show that models with similar benchmark scores can exhibit different internal representations, and that these differences predict accuracy and robustness across diverse spatial reasoning benchmarks. To isolate this bias from evaluation-set skew, we introduce SpatialTunnel, a synthetic benchmark designed to expose spatial shortcut biases by removing common correlations present in natural images. Experiments confirm that the entanglement is model-intrinsic, and that models with well-separated spatial axes exhibit greater robustness, suggesting that well-structured spatial representations lead to more reliable spatial reasoning across diverse benchmarks. Code and benchmark are available on the project page: https://cheolhong0916.github.io/whyfarlooksup.github.io/.


### [40] [LiveSVG: Zero-Shot SVG Animation via Video Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30174)
*Matan Levy, Ran Margolin, Bar Cavia, Dvir Samuel, Yael Pritch, Shmuel Peleg, Alex Rav Acha, Ariel Shamir, Dani Lischinski*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
LiveSVG提出了一种零样本的SVG动画生成方法，通过冻结的图像到视频扩散模型生成目标视频，再结合可微渲染和双层运动表示（每组单应性矩阵加每路径贝塞尔控制点偏移）将原始SVG拟合到该视频上，无需骨架先验，在AniClipart和ChallengeSVG基准上显著优于现有方法。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有SVG动画方法在处理复杂运动时存在明显局限：基于LLM的代码合成无法表达精细的非刚性贝塞尔变形，而基于Score Distillation Sampling的方法提供噪声梯度且常需类别特定的骨架先验。作者旨在提出一种无需骨架、无需视频先验训练的零样本SVG动画生成方法，以支持复杂多物体场景中的精细变形。

**Method:** LiveSVG采用零样本流水线：首先输入SVG图像和运动提示，使用冻结的图像到视频扩散模型生成可预览的目标视频；然后通过可微渲染将原始SVG拟合到该视频上。拟合阶段无需骨架，采用双层运动表示——粗粒度层使用每组的单应性矩阵表示整体刚性运动，细粒度层使用每路径的贝塞尔控制点偏移表示局部变形。为解决像素级拟合中颜色带来的对应歧义，提出球体堆积重着色（sphere-packing recolorization）策略。同时构建了ChallengeSVG基准，包含复杂多物体场景。

**Result:** 在AniClipart和ChallengeSVG两个基准上的实验表明，LiveSVG显著优于现有SVG动画方法。ChallengeSVG基准专门设计了复杂多物体场景，暴露了先前方法的局限性，而LiveSVG在这些场景中仍能生成高质量、与提示对齐且完全可编辑的矢量动画。

**Conclusion:** LiveSVG验证了直接参考视频拟合作为SVG动画生成路线的实用性和鲁棒性，证明了无需类别先验、无需骨架即可实现精细贝塞尔变形动画的可行性。该方法为可编辑矢量动画提供了一种简洁而有效的零样本范式，未来可拓展至更复杂的动画控制场景。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
We introduce LiveSVG, a zero-shot approach for generating Scalable Vector Graphics (SVG) animations using video diffusion models. Current SVG animation methods struggle with complex motions: LLM-based code synthesis fails to express fine, non-rigid Bézier deformations, while Score Distillation Sampling (SDS) provides noisy gradients and often requires category-specific priors like skeletons. In contrast, LiveSVG fits vector geometry directly to an explicitly generated target video. Given an input SVG image and a motion prompt, we generate a previewable target video using a frozen image-to-video model, then fit the original SVG to this video via differentiable rendering. Our fitting stage is skeleton-free, utilizing a dual-level motion representation that combines per-group homographies for coarse articulation with per-path Bézier control-point offsets for local deformations. To resolve color-induced correspondence ambiguities during pixel-wise fitting, we introduce a novel sphere-packing recolorization strategy. We also present ChallengeSVG, a benchmark of complex, multi-object scenes that exposes the limitations of prior work. Evaluations demonstrate that LiveSVG significantly outperforms existing methods on both AniClipart and ChallengeSVG, establishing direct reference-video fitting as a practical, robust route to prompt-aligned and fully editable vector animation.


### [41] [IP-Adapter Is All You Need: Towards Fine-Tuning-Free Diffusion-Based Talking Face Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30230)
*Hao Wu, Xiangyang Luo, Hao Wang, Jiawei Zhang, Yi Zhang, Jinwei Wang*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文提出一种无需微调的扩散模型框架，利用预训练的Stable Diffusion和IP-Adapter直接生成说话人脸视频，并设计了三个无训练参数的模块（Structurist、Structure Controller、Noise Sensor）解决身份漂移、同步误差和时间不稳定问题，在唇同步精度和视觉保真度上超越现有最优方法。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有基于扩散模型的说话人脸生成方法仍依赖任务特定的微调和大规模音视频数据集，导致计算成本高昂，限制了扩散方法在社区中的可扩展性和可访问性，亟需一种无需微调的高效范式。

**Method:** 提出一种免微调范式，直接利用预训练的Stable Diffusion和IP-Adapter进行说话人脸生成；同时设计了三个无训练参数的组件：Structurist显式解耦并重组唇部和外观特征以缓解身份漂移和外观失真，Structure Controller基于准单调运动趋势自适应优化嵌入以实现精确唇同步，Noise Sensor引入高斯先验检测并抑制闪烁和抖动伪影以增强时间一致性。

**Result:** 实验结果表明，该方法在唇同步精度（PCLD至少提升0.16）和视觉保真度（FID至少改善0.7）上均超越现有最先进方法，验证了免微调扩散框架在说话人脸生成中的有效性。

**Conclusion:** 该研究建立了一种新颖的免微调扩散框架，证明了无需任务特定微调即可利用预训练模型实现高质量说话人脸生成的可行性，为降低扩散模型在该任务中的计算开销和提升可扩展性提供了新思路。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
With the rapid advancement of diffusion models, talking face generation has made remarkable progress. However, existing diffusion-based methods still require task-specific fine-tuning and large-scale audiovisual datasets, resulting in high computational costs that hinder scalability and accessibility of diffusion-based approaches across the research community. To address this, we propose a finetuning-free paradigm that directly performs talking face generation using the pretrained weights of Stable Diffusion and IP-Adapter. This backbone leverages the visual embedding capability of IP-Adapter to mine lip-related semantics from the pretrained Stable Diffusion. To address the challenges of identity drift, synchronization errors, and temporal instability, we also design three trainable-parameterfree components: (1) the Structurist, which explicitly disentangles and reassembles lip and appearance features to mitigate identity drift and appearance distortion; (2) the Structure Controller, which adaptively refines embeddings based on quasi-monotonic motion trends for precise lip synchronization; and (3) the Noise Sensor, which introduces Gaussian prior to detect and suppress flicker and jitter artifacts and enhance temporal consistency. Experimental results show that our method outperforms existing SOTA approaches in both lip-sync accuracy (at least 0.16 gain in PCLD) and visual fidelity (at least 0.7 improvement in FID), establishing a novel fine-tuning-free diffusion framework for talking face generation.


### [42] [Beyond 3D VQAs: Injecting 3D Spatial Priors into Vision-Language Models for Enhanced Geometric Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30231)
*Chun-Hsiao Yeh, Shengyi Qian, Manchen Wang, Yi Ma, Joseph Tighe, Fanyi Xiao*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文提出GASP框架，通过将几何先验（点对应和深度一致性）注入LLM的Transformer层来增强VLM的3D空间推理能力，无需3D VQA训练数据即可在空间基准上取得显著提升。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有VLM在处理鲁棒的3D空间推理时表现不佳，微调3D VQA数据集会导致过拟合数据集特定偏差，而集成专用3D视觉编码器则缺乏灵活性和可扩展性。本文指出真正的空间理解应源于学习基础几何先验，而非仅依赖高层VQA监督信号。

**Method:** GASP框架通过在LLM的Transformer所有层施加一个轻量级对应头（correspondence head）作为深度监督信号，并利用大规模视频场景中的真实几何信息进行双目标训练：对比损失基于真实点对应强制2D视角不变性，深度一致性监督则解决3D几何歧义问题。

**Result:** 标准VLM内部的对应匹配准确率通常低于5%，而GASP训练后峰值逐层对应率提升至超过70%，时间鲁棒性维持在85%以上（基线低于5%）。在下游空间基准上，GASP在All-Angles Bench上提升18.2%，在VSI-Bench上提升29.0%，且完全无需3D VQA训练数据。

**Conclusion:** 实验结果表明，从基础几何先验中学习是使VLM获得更可靠3D空间推理能力的一种有前景且可泛化的路径，该方法有效规避了传统依赖3D VQA数据微调的过拟合问题，并为VLM的空间智能提供了更底层且更通用的训练范式。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Vision-Language Models (VLMs) often struggle with robust 3D spatial reasoning. Prevailing methods that rely on fine-tuning with 3D visual question-answering (VQA) datasets may overfit dataset-specific biases, while integrating specialized 3D visual encoders is often inflexible and cumbersome. In this paper, we argue that genuine spatial understanding should emerge from learning fundamental geometric priors, not only from high-level VQA supervision. We propose GASP (Geometric-Aware Spatial Priors), a framework that injects these priors directly into the LLM's transformer layers. GASP employs a small correspondence head, applied as a deep supervision signal across all layers, and is trained with a dual objective leveraging ground-truth geometry from large-scale video scenes: a contrastive loss on ground-truth point correspondences enforces 2D view-invariance, while a depth consistency supervision resolves 3D geometric ambiguities. Our analysis first provides a diagnostic showing that standard VLMs' internal correspondence matching accuracy is very low (often below 5%). We then demonstrate that our training substantially improves this behavior, boosting peak layer-wise correspondence to over 70% and maintaining over 85% temporal robustness while baselines remain below 5%. These internal improvements translate to significant gains on downstream spatial benchmarks including +18.2% on All-Angles Bench and +29.0% on VSI-Bench, all without training on any 3D VQA data. Our findings indicate that learning from fundamental geometric priors is a promising and generalizable pathway towards VLMs with more reliable 3D spatial reasoning.


### [43] [VideoFDB: Evaluating Full-Duplex Vision-Speech Capabilities in Conversational Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30256)
*Amrita Mazumdar, Seonwook Park, Rajarshi Roy, Nikhil Srihari, Shengze Wang, Yuhao Zhou, Julia Wang, Koki Nagano, Shalini De Mello*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
VideoFDB 是首个针对全双工视听到视听（AV2AV）对话智能体的基准测试，包含237个真实视频通话片段、11种非语言对话动态的标注及基于评分规则的LM-as-Judge评估框架，实验揭示现有系统存在描述性崩溃、视觉流忽略等系统性缺陷，且级联语音到虚拟形象系统架构根本上无法产生全双工非语言线索。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 自然的人机对话本质上应是全双工且视听双模态的，智能体需要同时理解和产生语言及非语言线索（如点头、微笑、手势），然而现有的全双工基准仅评估语音模态，缺乏对视听全双工交互能力的系统性评测，这阻碍了下一代多模态对话智能体的发展。

**Method:** VideoFDB 从真实视频通话中收集了237个双人对话片段，覆盖11种非语言对话动态；提出将感知行为与生成行为分离的分类体系；并设计了一套基于评分规则的LM-as-Judge评估框架，通过可解释的评估轴衡量对话质量对非语言动态的建模能力。研究还对比了开闭源视觉-语音智能体以及级联语音到虚拟形象系统。

**Result:** 实验发现现有系统存在两类系统性失败模式：描述性崩溃（captioning collapse）和视觉流忽略（visual-stream ignorance）；当前系统仅能在显式视觉问答任务中利用视觉信息，而无法在自然对话所需的流式联合视听接地（streaming joint audiovisual grounding）中持续利用视觉流；级联式语音到虚拟形象系统的架构从根本上无法产生全双工的非语言线索。

**Conclusion:** VideoFDB 作为首个全双工AV2AV交互基准，为系统性评估多模态对话智能体奠定了重要基础，揭示了当前模型在非语言动态建模上的根本性局限，有望加速下一代全双工视听对话智能体的研发。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Natural human conversation is full-duplex and audio-visual: people simultaneously speak and listen while continuously interpreting and producing nonverbal cues, such as nods, smiles, and gestures. To support successful human-agent interaction, agents must model full-duplex audiovisual conversation; however, existing full-duplex benchmarks evaluate only speech. In this work, we present VideoFDB, the first benchmark to evaluate full-duplex audio-visual-to-audio-visual (AV2AV) conversational agents. VideoFDB contributes (i) 237 dyadic clips spanning 11 nonverbal conversational dynamics from real-world video calls, (ii) a taxonomy separating perception from generation behaviors, and (iii) a rubric-based LM-as-judge evaluation framework with interpretable axes for assessing conversational quality with respect to nonverbal conversational dynamics. Across open- and closed-source vision-speech agents, we find systematic failure modes: captioning collapse and visual-stream ignorance, and we show that current systems exploit vision for explicit visual question answering but not for the streaming joint audiovisual grounding required in natural conversation. We further evaluate cascaded speech-to-avatar systems and find that their architecture fundamentally precludes the production of full-duplex nonverbal cues. As the first benchmark for full-duplex AV2AV interaction, VideoFDB establishes a foundation for systematic evaluation and, we hope, will accelerate the advancement and development of next-generation multimodal conversational agents.


### [44] [Stable-Layers: Fine-Tuning Image Layer Decomposition Models with VLM-Scored Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30257)
*Ciara Rowles, Reshinth Adithyan, Nikhil Pinnaparaju, Vikram Voleti, Mark Boss*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
Stable-Layers 提出一种无需成对监督的强化学习框架，利用视觉语言模型的反馈对预训练层分解模型进行微调，通过两阶段评估管道解决奖励信号方差不足的问题，在 Crello 数据集上显著提升了层分离质量和重建精度。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有层分解模型通常依赖成对监督数据训练，而获取高质量逐层标注成本高昂；直接使用 VLM 作为奖励信号进行强化学习时，VLM 在孤立评分场景下易将评判压缩到狭窄区间，导致 GRPO 算法因组内方差不足而难以有效学习，这是该研究要解决的核心问题。

**Method:** Stable-Layers 基于 Qwen-Image-Layered 预训练模型，采用 Flow-GRPO 与 LoRA 适配相结合的强化学习框架：对每张图像采样多个候选分解，使用 VLM 进行评分，并从组内相对优势中优化策略。关键创新在于两阶段评估管道：第一阶段对每个候选样本进行五项编辑中心指标的独立评分，第二阶段通过网格校准让 VLM 对所有候选进行并排重新评分，从而增强奖励信号的区分度。

**Result:** 在 Crello 数据集上，Stable-Layers 相比基线模型获得了更强的层分离效果，减少了空白层或伪影过多的层，并降低了逐层重建误差。

**Conclusion:** 本研究表明，通过精心设计的奖励校准机制，可以仅利用 VLM 反馈而非成对监督来有效微调层分解模型，为减少对标注数据依赖的图像分解任务提供了可行的强化学习范式。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
We present Stable-Layers, a reinforcement learning framework that eliminates the need for paired supervision by fine-tuning a pretrained layer decomposition model using only feedback from a vision-language model (VLM). Starting from Qwen-Image-Layered, we apply Flow-GRPO with LoRA adaptation, sampling multiple candidate decompositions per image, scoring them with a VLM, and optimising the policy from group-relative advantages. The key challenge lies in designing a reliable reward signal: VLMs scoring samples in isolation tend to compress their judgements into a narrow band, leaving GRPO with little within-group variance to learn from. We address this with a two-stage evaluation pipeline that pairs structured per-sample scoring across five edit-centric criteria with a grid-based calibration step in which the VLM re-scores all candidates side-by-side. Stable-Layers produces decompositions with stronger layer separation, fewer blank or artifact-heavy layers, and lower per-layer reconstruction error on the Crello dataset compared to the base model.


### [45] [LoMo: Local Modality Substitution for Deeper Vision-Language Fusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30265)
*Feng Han, Zhixiong Zhang, Zheming Liang, Yibin Wang, Jiaqi Wang*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文发现视觉-语言模型（VLM）中存在的“载体敏感性”问题——即文本问题替换为图像后会引发严重性能下降，并归因于训练数据中文本与图像不对称的角色分配。为此提出LoMo（局部模态替换），一种轻量级、架构无关的数据整理范式，通过将单模态提示重构为交错多模态序列，对语义等价的文本与图像载体施加跨模态表征不变性监督，在13个多模态基准上平均提升2.6–2.8个点。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有VLM在文本和图像承载相同语义信息时表现出严重的不一致性：将文本问题替换为渲染图像后性能急剧下降。作者将此“载体敏感性”问题归因于训练语料中文本与图像被组织为非对称角色（文本作为语言查询、图像作为视觉参考），导致模型对不同模态的信息获取产生偏好，无法对齐语义等价内容在文字载体与视觉载体之间的表征。

**Method:** 提出LoMo（Local Modality Substitution），一种轻量级、架构无关的数据整理范式。它通过将单模态提示（如纯文本问题）动态选择目标文本片段并将其重新编码为渲染图像，重构为“文本-图像-文本”交错多模态序列，从而在保持语义等价的前提下对同一内容在不同载体（文字/图像）上的表征提供跨模态不变性监督。

**Result:** 在13个多模态基准上的大量实验表明，LoMo显著提升了多模态推理能力与跨模态融合深度。在LLaVA-OneVision-1.5-8B上相比标准SFT提升2.67个点，在Qwen3.5-9B上提升2.82个点，且在不同基础模型上表现出一致的改进。

**Conclusion:** 研究表明训练数据中的模态角色不对称性是导致VLM载体敏感性的根本原因，LoMo通过数据层面的跨模态表征对齐有效缓解了这一问题，为提升VLM在多模态推理中的鲁棒性和泛化能力提供了一种简单有效的方案。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Vision-Language Models (VLMs) have achieved substantial progress across a wide range of understanding and reasoning tasks, driven by large-scale image-text training aimed at multimodal fusion. Ideally, replacing a textual question with its rendered-image counterpart should leave model performance essentially unaffected. In practice, however, such modality substitution induces dramatic performance degradation. We attribute this "carrier sensitivity" issue to an inherent bias in current training corpora. Across prevalent datasets such as image captioning, VQA, OCR, and web-sourced interleaved data, text and images are typically organized into distinct and asymmetric roles, with text serving as linguistic queries and images as visual references. Such data bias leads VLMs to exhibit distinct preferences for information acquisition across different modalities. Consequently, VLMs fail to align representations of semantically equivalent content across textual and visual carriers, making model reasoning fragile under modality substitution. To address this, we propose Local Modality Substitution (LoMo), a lightweight, architecture-agnostic data curation paradigm designed to provide supervision for cross-modal representational invariance between semantically equivalent text and image carriers. LoMo achieves this by reformulating single-modality prompts into seamlessly interleaved multimodal sequences. It dynamically selects target text spans and recasts them as rendered images, thereby preserving the same semantics across "text, visual, text" carriers. Extensive experiments across 13 diverse multimodal benchmarks demonstrate that LoMo significantly improves overall multimodal reasoning and yields deeper cross-modal fusion. Specifically, it delivers consistent gains across foundational models, improving over standard SFT by 2.67 points on LLaVA-OneVision-1.5-8B and 2.82 points on Qwen3.5-9B.


### [46] [Grounded 3D-Aware Spatial Vision-Language Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30307)
*An-Chieh Cheng, Yang Fu, Yatai Ji, Ligeng Zhu, Guanqi Zhan, Zhuoyang Zhang, Zhaojing Yang, Song Han, Yao Lu, Pavlo Molchanov, Vidya Nariyambut Murali, Jan Kautz, Xiaolong Wang, Hongxu Yin, Sifei Liu*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
GR3D是一个统一框架的空间视觉语言模型，同时具备显式2D定位、隐式2D定位和单目3D定位三种互补能力，通过将定位作为归纳偏置来增强VLM的空间理解能力，在多种空间基准上取得了一致改进。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有视觉语言模型在空间理解方面存在不足，缺乏一种统一的框架来同时处理2D定位、隐式引用和单目3D定位等多种空间理解任务，且定位能力本身是否能够作为归纳偏置来提升VLM的泛化空间理解能力尚未被充分探索。

**Method:** GR3D提出了一个统一框架，包含三种定位能力：显式2D定位、隐式2D定位和单目3D定位。隐式定位机制在生成过程中自动识别实体提及并插入对应区域token到文本流中，使模型在生成空间思维链响应时能实时引用视觉证据；区域提示的单目3D定位设计则基于定位后的区域查询预测相机视图中的3D边界框，并采用内参感知归一化和密集几何监督来提升3D预测精度。

**Result:** GR3D在多种空间基准上取得了 consistent improvements，包括有定位和无定位的空间理解任务，证明了定位作为归纳偏置能够有效增强VLM的空间理解能力，且这些定位能力对超越定位任务本身的通用空间理解也有提升作用。

**Conclusion:** 该研究表明，将显式2D、隐式2D和单目3D定位能力统一集成到VLM中是一种有效的设计策略，定位作为一种归纳偏置能够系统性增强模型的空间理解能力，为开发更强大的空间感知视觉语言模型提供了新方向。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
We present GR3D, a spatial vision language model equipped with three complementary grounding capabilities--explicit 2D grounding, implicit 2D grounding, and monocular 3D grounding--within a single framework. GR3D introduces an implicit grounding mechanism that identifies entity mentions during generation and inserts the corresponding region tokens into the text stream, allowing the model to reference visual evidence on the fly when producing spatial chain-of-thought responses. In parallel, a region-prompted monocular 3D grounding design predicts 3D bounding boxes in the camera view from grounded region queries, supported by intrinsic-aware normalization and dense geometric supervision. Together, these grounding capabilities enable GR3D to decompose complex spatial understanding problems into grounded 2D perception followed by 3D inference. GR3D achieves consistent improvements across grounded and non-grounded spatial benchmarks, demonstrating grounding as an effective inductive bias for strengthening spatial understanding in VLMs. These grounding capabilities collectively enhance general spatial understanding beyond the grounding task itself.


### [47] [GPIC: A Giant Permissive Image Corpus for Visual Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30341)
*Keshigeyan Chandrasegaran, Kyle Sargent, Suchir Agarwal, Michael Jang, Michael Poli, Juan Carlos Niebles, Justin Johnson, Jiajun Wu, Li Fei-Fei*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
GPIC是一个约28万亿像素的大规模许可图像数据集，包含1亿训练样本，均采用视觉语言模型标注，并附带基准测试协议和像素空间流匹配基线模型，兼具研究用途和商业用途的开放性。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 视觉生成建模的可扩展方法研究需要大规模、易获取且稳定的数据集，现有数据集在规模、许可合规性和标准化评估协议方面存在不足，限制了研究的可复现性和商业转化。

**Method:** GPIC收集了约28万亿像素的互联网图像，使用最先进的视觉语言模型为其生成标题，经过安全过滤和去重处理，并托管于Hugging Face平台。数据集划分为1亿训练样本、20万验证样本和100万测试样本。论文同时提供了生成建模的基准测试协议，并构建了像素空间流匹配的参考基线模型。

**Result:** 构建了包含约28万亿像素、1亿训练样本的大规模许可图像数据集GPIC；所有图像均获得研究和商业用途许可；提供了标准化基准测试协议和像素空间流匹配基线模型的结果；数据集、基准和模型已在Hugging Face和Stanford网站公开。

**Conclusion:** GPIC为视觉生成建模研究提供了一个大规模、许可开放、经过安全过滤和去重的标准化数据集与评估平台，有望推动生成式模型在可扩展性、可复现性和商业应用方面的发展。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Studying scalable methods for visual generative modeling requires large, accessible, and stable datasets. We introduce GPIC, a Giant Permissive Image Corpus of approximately 28 trillion pixels. GPIC comprises diverse internet images captioned by a state-of-the-art vision-language model, including 100M training, 200K validation, and 1M test examples. Moreover, all GPIC images are permissively licensed for both research and commercial use. GPIC is safety-filtered, deduplicated, and centrally hosted on Hugging Face. We provide a benchmarking protocol for generative modeling on GPIC. Finally, we provide a reference baseline for pixel-space flow matching on GPIC. Our dataset, benchmark, and models are available at https://huggingface.co/datasets/stanford-vision-lab/gpic. Evaluation toolkit and code are available at https://gpic.stanford.edu


### [48] [YoCausal: How Far is Video Generation from World Model? A Causality Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30346)
*You-Zhe Xie, Yu-Hsuan Li, Jie-Ying Lee, Kaipeng Zhang, Yu-Lun Liu, Zhixiang Wang*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
YoCausal 提出了一种基于认知科学中期望违背范式的两层级基准，通过零成本时间反转真实视频作为自然反事实样本，用于评估视频扩散模型对因果关系的理解，揭示了当前SOTA模型在真正因果推理与人类水平之间存在显著差距。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有视频扩散模型基准大多依赖合成数据，存在模拟到真实的泛化鸿沟，难以判断模型是真正理解因果关系还是仅过拟合统计时间模式，因此需要一个能评估真实世界中因果认知能力的基准。

**Method:** YoCausal 借鉴认知科学的期望违背范式，通过零成本时间反转真实视频构建自然反事实样本，建立可任意扩展的评估协议。第一层引入逆向惊奇指数（RSI），通过去噪损失量化模型对时间之箭的感知能力；第二层引入因果关系认知指数（CCI），利用视觉语言模型将数据集分层为因果与非因果子集，从而将真正的因果推理与时间偏差分离。

**Result:** 对13个最先进的视频扩散模型的评估表明，模型能够感知时间箭头方向并不意味着具备因果理解能力，并且所有模型在因果认知上与人类水平存在显著差距。

**Conclusion:** 该研究揭示了当前视频扩散模型在因果推理方面的根本局限：时间感知与因果理解是分离的能力，仅靠统计时间模式学习不足以实现类人的因果认知，为未来世界模型的可信因果推理能力评估提供了新范式。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
As video diffusion models (VDMs) advance toward world models, a key question arises: do they truly understand causality, or merely overfit to statistical temporal patterns? Existing benchmarks mostly rely on synthetic data, limiting real-world generalization due to the sim-to-real gap. We present YoCausal, a two-level benchmark inspired by the Violation of Expectation (VoE) paradigm from cognitive science. By temporally reversing real-world videos at zero cost as natural counterfactual samples, YoCausal establishes an arbitrarily extensible evaluation protocol. Level 1 introduces the Reverse Surprise Index (RSI), quantifying arrow-of-time perception via denoising loss. Level 2 introduces the Causality Cognition Index (CCI), which leverages a VLM to stratify datasets into causal and non-causal subsets, disentangling genuine causal reasoning from temporal bias. Evaluation of 13 state-of-the-art VDMs reveals that perceiving the arrow of time does not imply understanding causality, and a significant gap persists relative to human-level causal cognition.

### [49] [RightNow-Arabic-0.5B-Turbo: An Open Sub-1B Arabic Language Model via Vocabulary Injection and Edge-First Deployment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28827)
*Jaber Jaber, Osama Jaber*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
RightNow-Arabic-0.5B-Turbo 是一个基于 Qwen2.5-0.5B 构建的 518M 参数阿拉伯语专用解码器 LLM，通过词嵌入扩展、持续预训练、指令微调、偏好优化和权重汤合并，在三个阿拉伯语基准上达到 35.9% 平均准确率，超越所有同类开源模型，且量化后仅 398 MB，在单张 H100 上达到 635 tokens/s 的推理速度。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有的开源阿拉伯语大语言模型存在明显空白：小于 1B 的多语言模型仅将阿拉伯语作为附带处理，性能不佳；而 7B–70B 的阿拉伯语专用模型需要服务器级硬件才能运行。唯一的 sub-2B 阿拉伯语专用模型 Kuwain-1.5B 未公开权重，导致该规模下缺乏可复现、可部署的开源阿拉伯语模型。

**Method:** 以 Qwen2.5-0.5B 为基座，通过平均子词初始化方法扩充 27,032 个阿拉伯语 token 的嵌入层；在 8×H100 上使用 FSDP、FlashAttention varlen packing 和 Liger fused kernels 在 5.04 亿阿拉伯语 token 上继续预训练；随后在 129,116 条阿拉伯语指令对上使用仅响应损失掩码进行监督微调，在 6,750 条阿拉伯语偏好对上执行直接偏好优化，并通过对三个检查点进行权重汤合并得到最终模型。

**Result:** 在 COPA-ar、Arabic HellaSwag 和 ArabicMMLU 三个基准上，合并模型达到 35.9% 平均准确率，超越所有同类开源模型；在 COPA-ar 上以 Falcon-H1-1.5B 三分之一的参数量取得相同成绩（58.4%），并以 1/18 的参数量恢复了 SILMA-9B 平均性能的 67%。边缘部署量化至 q4_k_m 仅 398 MB，在单张 H100 上 batch size=1 时通过 llama.cpp 达到 635 tokens/s。

**Conclusion:** 该研究表明，通过精心设计的 token 嵌入扩展、高效的持续预训练和后训练策略，可以在极小规模（0.5B 参数）上构建出性能可用的阿拉伯语专用模型，弥合了超小模型与大型阿拉伯语模型之间的差距。全部代码、权重及量化版本已开源，为资源受限场景下的阿拉伯语 NLP 提供了实用的轻量级方案。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Open Arabic large language models split into two classes: sub-1B multilingual models that treat Arabic as an afterthought (Qwen2.5-0.5B, Falcon-H1-0.5B), and 7B-70B Arabic-specialized models that require a server to run (Jais, AceGPT, ALLaM, SILMA). The one published attempt at a sub-2B Arabic-specialized model, Kuwain-1.5B, never released its weights. We present RightNow-Arabic-0.5B-Turbo, a 518M-parameter Arabic-specialized decoder LLM built on Qwen2.5-0.5B. The pipeline adds 27,032 Arabic tokens via mean-subtoken initialization, continues pretraining on 504M Arabic tokens on 8xH100 with FSDP, FlashAttention varlen packing, and Liger fused kernels, then applies supervised fine-tuning on 129,116 Arabic instruction pairs with response-only loss masking, direct preference optimization on 6,750 Arabic preference pairs, and weight soup merging across three checkpoints. On three lm-evaluation-harness Arabic benchmarks (COPA-ar, Arabic HellaSwag, ArabicMMLU) the merged model reaches 35.9% mean accuracy, beats every same-class open model, ties Falcon-H1-1.5B on COPA-ar (58.4%) at one-third the size, and recovers 67% of SILMA-9B's mean at 1/18 the parameters. The edge build quantizes to 398 MB (q4_k_m) and delivers 635 tokens/s at batch size 1 on a single H100 via llama.cpp. All code (5,555 lines across 25 scripts), weights (bf16, int8, and four GGUF quantizations), and benchmark scripts are released at https://huggingface.co/RightNowAI/RightNow-Arabic-0.5B-Turbo.


### [50] [GenesisFunc: Multi-Agent Data Generation for Accurate and Generalizable Function-Calling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28835)
*Hao-Xiang Xu, Chong Deng, Jiaqing Liu, Wen Wang, Qian Chen, Lujia Bao, Xiangang Li, Zhen-Hua Ling*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
GenesisFunc 是一种自动化函数调用训练数据生成管线，采用多智能体框架和多阶段评估系统，从公开基准中提取可靠 API 并生成高质量、多样化的对话数据；在 8B 模型上微调后，其函数调用能力在域内和域外均超越同规模开源模型，且可媲美部分最新 API 模型。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 大语言模型的函数调用能力高度依赖高质量、多样且覆盖广泛场景的训练数据，然而真实世界函数调用数据的获取与标注非常困难，现有合成管线常存在 API 不可靠、工具可扩展性有限、数据多样性不足以及质量控制薄弱等问题，亟需一种自动、可靠且可扩展的数据生成方法。

**Method:** GenesisFunc 设计了一条自动化管线，首先从公开基准中提取可靠的工具 API，然后利用多智能体框架驱动对话生成系统，产生覆盖多种场景的多样化交互数据，并在整个过程中通过多阶段评估系统对生成数据的准确性进行反复验证和质量控制。

**Result:** 基于合成数据微调的 8B 模型在域内函数调用性能和域外泛化能力上均优于同类规模的开源模型，且其函数调用能力可达到与部分最新基于 API 的模型相当的水平；该方法在下游工具上也展现出良好的可扩展性，验证了其实用性。

**Conclusion:** GenesisFunc 通过自动化、高质量的数据生成管线有效解决了函数调用训练数据构建的瓶颈，证明了合成数据可以支撑小模型达到接近商用 API 模型的函数调用能力，为 LLM 工具使用能力的规模化训练提供了可行且可扩展的路径。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) extend their capabilities through function-calling (FC), which relies on training data with high quality, diversity, and broad coverage of scenario. However, obtaining and annotating real function-calling data is challenging, while synthetic data from existing pipelines often suffers from unreliable APIs, limited tool scalability, insufficient diversity, and weak quality control. To address these, we present GenesisFunc, an automated pipeline for generating FC training data. Starting from reliable tools in widely used public benchmarks, our GenesisFunc employs a multi-agent framework to support a dialogue generation system that produces conversations spanning diverse scenarios, while maintaining both diversity and quality throughout the process. The accuracy of the data is further reinforced through a multi-stage evaluation system. We fine-tune an 8B LLM on the synthetic dataset and show through extensive experiments that it outperforms similarly sized open-source models in in-domain FC performance and out-of-domain generalization, while reaching FC capabilities comparable to some of the latest API-based models. In addition, our method demonstrates strong potential to scale effectively across downstream tools, underscoring its real-world applicability.


### [51] [No Reader Left Behind: Multi-Agent Summaries Everyone Can Understand](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28836)
*Jimin Jung, MyoungJin Kim, Jaehyung Seo, Heuiseok Lim*

#### 🧩 TL;DR

#### 📘 Detailed Summary

**Method:** NRLB（No Reader Left Behind）是一个多智能体框架，模拟三类代表性读者群体（小学生、非母语者、注意力缺陷读者），采用模板化规划与迭代式面向读者优化的结合策略，实现对困难术语、缺失上下文和歧义句子的系统性检测与修正。

**Result:** 在多个数据集上的评估表明，NRLB在保持事实准确性的同时一致性地提升了摘要可读性；人工评估中，标注者偏好率介于55%至76%之间，验证了其生成平实语言摘要的有效性。

**Conclusion:** NRLB通过多智能体模拟不同读者群体的认知需求，为生成既忠于原文又广泛可访问的平实语言摘要提供了可行框架，彰显了其在面向普通公众的文本简化与摘要生成领域的应用潜力。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
The Plain Writing Act in the United States requires government documents to be accessible in clear and simple language that the general public can easily understand, yet existing summarization systems struggle to address diverse linguistic and cognitive barriers among general readers. We present NRLB (No Reader Left Behind), a multi-agent framework for plain language summarization that simulates three representative reader groups: elementary school student readers, non-native readers, and readers with attention deficits. NRLB combines template-based planning with iterative, reader-oriented refinement, enabling systematic detection and resolution of difficult terms, missing contexts, and confusing sentences. Evaluations across multiple datasets demonstrate consistent improvements in readability while preserving factual accuracy. Human evaluation further validates NRLB's impact, with annotator preference rates ranging from 55% to 76%, highlighting NRLB's potential to produce plain language summaries that are both faithful to the source and broadly accessible to the general public.


### [52] [SERC: LDPC-Inspired Semantic Error Correction for Retrieval-Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28837)
*Gyumin Kim, Juhwan Park, Jaeha Kim, Seunggyun Han, Kyungrak Son, Ikbeom Jang*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
提出基于LDPC码启发的语义纠错框架SERC，将文本生成建模为语义噪声信道，通过生成稀疏验证查询并对照外部证据来高效检测和纠正LLM幻觉，无需训练且与模型无关，在多个基准上超越内省自纠正和强检索增强方法。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 大型语言模型存在显著的幻觉问题，现有内省式自纠正方法因自偏置而难以识别自身生成内容中的错误，缺乏外部验证机制，且传统密集验证方法开销过大，亟需一种高效、无需训练且与模型无关的幻觉缓解方案。

**Method:** 提出语义纠错框架SERC，将文本生成过程重新建模为语义噪声信道，将生成响应视为经噪声污染的码字。受低密度奇偶校验码启发，SERC采用稀疏验证策略：不穷举检查所有事实，而是生成低密度验证查询，并对照外部证据进行验证，实现高效的错误检测与纠正。

**Result:** 在LongForm Bio和TruthfulQA基准上使用Llama-3-8B和Qwen2.5-14B进行实验，SERC在事实精确度（FactScore）上显著超越内省自纠正方法和强检索增强基线，且使小型语言模型在幻觉减少和信息保留方面超越更大规模的基线模型。

**Conclusion:** SERC提供了一种无需训练、与模型无关的解决方案，相比密集验证方法显著降低了验证开销，在资源受限环境中实现了成本与保真度的最优权衡，为LLM幻觉缓解提供了理论化框架和实用方法。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
While Large Language Models (LLMs) have demonstrated remarkable capabilities, their reliability is significantly compromised by hallucinations. Existing intrinsic self-correction methods attempt to address this, but often fail due to self-bias, where models struggle to identify errors in their own outputs without external verification. To overcome these limitations, we propose the LDPC-inspired semantic error correction for retrieval-augmented generation (SERC), providing a theoretical framework to interpret and mitigate LLM hallucinations. We reformulate the text generation process as a semantic noisy channel, treating generated responses as noise-corrupted codewords. Inspired by low-density parity-check (LDPC) codes, SERC employs a sparse verification strategy: instead of exhaustively checking all facts, it generates low-density verification queries and validates them against external evidence to efficiently detect and correct errors. We evaluate SERC on LongForm Bio and TruthfulQA benchmarks using Llama-3-8B and Qwen2.5-14B. Experimental results demonstrate that SERC outperforms both intrinsic self-correction methods and strong retrieval-augmented baselines, demonstrating significant gains especially in factual precision (FactScore). Notably, SERC enables small language models (SLMs) to surpass the performance of larger baselines in hallucination reduction and information preservation. Our findings demonstrate that SERC provides a training-free, model-agnostic solution that significantly reduces verification overhead compared to dense methods, achieving an optimal trade-off between cost and fidelity in resource-constrained environments.


### [53] [How Consistent Are LLM Agents? Measuring Behavioral Reproducibility in Multi-Step Tool-Calling Pipelines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28840)
*Abel Yagubyan*

#### 🧩 TL;DR

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 尽管具备工具调用能力的大语言模型代理已广泛部署，但一个关键的可信性问题——同一代理在相同输入下是否表现出相同行为——尚未得到充分探索，现有关于一致性的研究主要针对ReAct风格的搜索型代理，而本文聚焦于包含类型化参数和有副作用的结构化工具调用场景。

**Method:** 本文提出了一个系统性实证研究框架，通过重复完全相同的一次次调用，测量多步骤工具调用型代理是否在工具选择、调用顺序和参数上保持一致，研究对象为结构化工具调用接口，区别于以往以自由文本动作为主的搜索型代理。

**Result:** 实验结果表明，在多步骤工具调用场景下，代理在相同的输入条件下反复执行时，在工具选择、调用顺序以及参数取值上均表现出明显的行为不一致性，揭示了当前工具调用型LLM代理在可靠性方面的潜在风险。

**Conclusion:** 本文揭示了部署在真实生产环境中的工具调用型LLM代理存在严重的行为不一致问题，强调了提升这类代理可靠性的重要性，并为未来研究提供了方向性的实证基础。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Large language model (LLM) agents with tool-calling capabilities are increasingly deployed in production systems, yet a fundamental reliability question remains under-explored: does the same agent behave the same way twice? We present a systematic empirical study of behavioral consistency in multi-step tool-calling agents, measuring whether agents select the same tools, in the same order, with the same arguments, across repeated identical invocations. Unlike prior work on consistency in ReAct-style agents(search-only, free-text actions), we study the richer setting of structured tool-calling interfaces with typed parameters and consequential side effects.


### [54] [Thoughts-as-Planning: Latent World Models for Chain-of-Thoughts Optimization via Reinforcement Planning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28842)

#### 🧩 TL;DR
提出Thoughts-as-Planning框架，将推理链优化形式化为语义潜空间上的序贯决策过程，通过构建潜在世界模型和保近嵌入空间，支持多尺度抽象推理链编辑，在多个语言任务上超越现有基线并提升可解释性。

#### 📘 Detailed Summary

**Result:** 在语言理解与生成任务上的大量实验表明，Thoughts-as-Planning在效率、鲁棒性和泛化性上均优于当前最优的推理链调优基线方法，同时通过结构化规划轨迹提供可解释性。

#### 📄 Abstract
The success of large language models (LLMs) across diverse NLP tasks has elevated the importance of reasoning chain optimization as a critical step in aligning model behavior with task objectives. Existing reasoning chain tuning methods often rely on black-box heuristics or gradient-free search, which lack interpretability, generalization, and sample efficiency. In this work, we introduce \textbf{Thoughts-as-Planning}, a novel framework that formalizes reasoning chain optimization as a sequential decision-making process over a latent semantic space. We model the LLM as a partially observable environment and learn a latent world model that simulates the effect of reasoning chain edits on downstream outputs. A proximity-preserving embedding space is constructed to encode reasoning chain-response dynamics, enabling planning via gradient descent or reinforcement learning. Our method supports multi-scale abstraction, allowing reasoning chain edits at token, segment, and instruction levels to be integrated into a unified planner. Through extensive experiments on language understanding and generation tasks, we demonstrate that Thoughts-as-Planning outperforms state-of-the-art reasoning chain tuning baselines in efficiency, robustness, and generalization, while offering interpretability through its structured planning trajectory. Our code is available at https://github.com/FastLM/Thoughts-as-Planning.

#### 📄 Abstract

Specifically, we introduce a novel chart-to-dictionary auxiliary task, offering a more flexible representation compared to traditional chart-to-table methods, making it particularly well-suited for integration with the Program-of-Thought (PoT) strategy. Experimental results demonstrate our strategy performs on par with existing chart summarization methods across semantic and factual metrics. Code is available on https://anonymous.4open.science/r/ZeroShot-PoT-C2T-5A6B.


### [56] [GrowLoop: Self-Evolving Conversation Evaluation Seeded by Human](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28882)
*Yihang Lin, Yunze Gao, Zeyang Lin, Dongbo Li, Kun Peng, Chenglong Song, Yue Liu*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
GrowLoop 提出了一种自演进的对话评估系统，通过启发式学习与 Rubric-Case 共演化机制，在无需显式标注标准的情况下持续适应模型能力与人类期望的变化，在人类相似性评估上显著优于现有方法。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有大语言模型的人类相似性评估方法面临三大挑战：人类评判标准是难以显式表述的隐性知识、不同注释者之间既存在共识也存在合理分歧、以及"人类相似"的标准随模型能力与人类期望动态变化。专家标注基准、奖励模型和自演进基准等方法均无法同时解决这三个问题。

**Method:** GrowLoop 采用自演进评估框架，以极少量人工种子标注作为初始动力，通过 LLM 智能体进行启发式学习，迭代地提取和精炼评估准则（rubrics）。在人类标注者意见一致处要求人机一致性，在意见分歧处仅要求合理性；通过 Rubric-Case 共演化机制实现持续演进，当评估目标发生变化时通过新的种子进行扩展。

**Result:** 在开放对话的人类相似性评估任务中，GrowLoop 生成的准则在人类判断对齐度上大幅超越现有方法，并能发现注释者忽略的问题。构建的基准测试有效区分不同能力层级的模型，揭示模型的具体不足，同时具备对新场景的泛化能力和随模型进步的自适应能力。

**Conclusion:** GrowLoop 将基准测试范式从人工更新或难度扩展转向全面的、持续的自演进，为处理动态变化的评估标准提供了新路径，其工作表明隐性知识的显式化与评估系统的持续适应是实现可靠开放域对话评估的关键方向。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
With the rapid advancement of large language models, evaluating human-likeness in open-ended conversation has become increasingly important. However, human-likeness is a form of tacit knowledge that humans perceive intuitively, yet the underlying criteria resist explicit formulation. Human judgments vary widely, with strong agreement on some cases and legitimate disagreement on others. Meanwhile, the criteria behind human judgments remain implicit, leaving no clear basis for constructing cases. Further, what counts as human-like is not static, but evolving with model capability and human expectations. Despite progress in evaluation methods such as expert-authored benchmarks, Reward Models, and self-evolving benchmarks, none addresses all three challenges simultaneously. Therefore, we propose GrowLoop, a self-evolving conversation evaluation system that continuously adapts as models advance and scenarios shift. With minimal human seed annotations as the first mover, LLM agents iteratively extract and refine evaluation rubrics through Heuristic Learning. Human-AI agreement is required where annotators converge, while only plausibility is expected where they diverge. Moreover, the Rubric-Case co-evolution mechanism enables continuous evolution, expanded through new seeds when the evaluation target moves. Applied to human-likeness evaluation in open-ended conversation, the generated rubrics not only substantially outperform existing methods in alignment with human judgments, but also uncover issues that annotators overlook. The resulting benchmark effectively discriminates models across capability tiers and reveals where they fall short, while generalizing to new scenarios and adapting as models advance. Our work shifts the benchmarking paradigm from manual updates or difficulty scaling to comprehensive, continuous self-evolution.


### [57] [Beyond Recall: Behavioral Specification as an Interpretive Layer for AI Personalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28969)
*Aarik Gulaya*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文提出用表征准确性（representational accuracy）衡量AI系统对用户解释的忠实程度，通过行为规格（Behavioral Specification）将用户数据压缩为解释性模式作为语言模型上下文，在14个自传语料库上以约25倍上下文成本降低实现表征准确性提升，并证明人类-AI对齐依赖于对用户的准确表征。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** AI系统在代表人类做决策时，其决策必须与用户对齐，但现有方法缺乏一种可量化的指标来衡量系统对用户解释（interpretation）的忠实程度，且传统上下文提供方式（原始语料、提取事实或商业记忆系统）存在成本高或表征不准确的问题。

**Method:** 作者提出表征准确性（representational accuracy）作为统一度量，并将解释层操作化为行为规格（Behavioral Specification），其参考实现通过激进压缩用户数据为解释性模式，作为语言模型上下文。在14个公开自传语料库上，采用校准的5评委LLM评审团对保留的行为预测进行评分，测试规格独立使用及与全量原始语料、全量提取事实、四种商业记忆系统（Mem0、Letta、Supermemory、Zep）组合的效果。

**Result:** 行为规格在聚合层面提升了表征准确性，几乎消除了模型的不确定推诿（hedging），以约25倍更低的上下文成本恢复了原始语料的大部分性能；它将受试者提升至一个共同的预测水平，绝对提升幅度在预训练基线最低时最大；在需要解释的问题上提升最大，而在需要回忆的问题上可能产生干扰。

**Conclusion:** 表征准确性与召回（recall）是不同维度的能力，人类-AI对齐依赖于对用户的准确表征，而表征准确性使得这种对齐变得可测试，为构建真正个性化且忠实于用户的AI系统提供了理论框架和实用方法。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
If an AI agent makes decisions on a person's behalf, those decisions must align with its user. We introduce representational accuracy to measure how faithfully a system captures a person's interpretation. An interpretive layer is operationalized as a Behavioral Specification. Our reference implementation aggressively compresses a person's data into interpretive patterns, served as context to a language model. We evaluate the Specification on a prototype benchmark of held-out behavioral predictions scored by a calibrated 5-judge LLM panel. We test it independently and in composition with a range of context conditions: full raw corpus, full extracted facts, and four commercial memory systems (Mem0, Letta, Supermemory, Zep).
  Across 14 public-domain autobiographical corpora, the Specification lifts representational accuracy in aggregate and nearly eliminates model hedging. It recovers most of what the raw corpus delivers, at ~25x less context cost. The Specification lifts subjects toward a common predictive level regardless of pretraining baseline; the lift in absolute points is therefore largest where the baseline is lowest, suggesting the population of relevance is anyone not adequately represented in pretraining. Lift is greatest on interpretation-required questions, where providing an interpretive layer enables model behavior that extracted facts or raw corpus do not. Conversely, on recall-required questions, this layer can interfere rather than help.
  We conclude that representational accuracy is distinct from recall and that human-AI alignment is dependent on how accurately the user is represented. Representational accuracy makes that alignment testable.


### [58] [Bosses, Kings, and the Commons: Cooperation Under Power Asymmetry in LLM Societies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29062)
*Abhilekh Borah*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文提出SovSim框架，用于模拟大型语言模型（LLM）社会在非对称权力结构下的公共资源治理行为，发现引入非对称权力（如老板/国王）会导致合作与可持续性严重崩溃，相较对称情境生存率最多下降87.3%。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现实中的公共资源（如渔业、森林、灌溉系统）常处于非对称权力结构下，部分个体或机构对资源提取拥有不成比例的控制权，但现有LLM社会模拟评估大多忽略了这种权力不对称，缺乏对LLM社会在非对称治理情境下行为的研究。

**Method:** SovSim是一个生成式多智能体模拟框架，在由对称智能体（工人/农民）组成的社会中引入一个具有非对称权力的智能体（老板/国王），所有智能体从共享资源中提取资源，共同决定资源的长期可持续性，并在十一个最先进的LLM模型上进行实验。

**Result:** 实验发现，引入非对称权力后，LLM社会的合作与可持续性出现严重崩溃，相较于对称设置，生存率下降最多达87.3%。

**Conclusion:** 研究表明权力不对称会显著破坏LLM社会中的合作与资源可持续性，揭示了现有LLM治理模拟忽略权力结构的局限性，为合成治理仿真中引入更现实的社会结构提供了重要启示。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Communities can sustainably manage shared resources (commons) through self-governance and cooperative norms, a central finding of Ostrom's theory of self-governance. However, real-world commons (e.g., fisheries, forests, and irrigation systems) are often governed under asymmetric power structures, where certain individuals or institutions possess disproportionate control over resource extraction and collective outcomes. As Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly explored as agents in synthetic governance simulations, understanding how LLM societies behave under asymmetric power structures is becoming increasingly important, yet existing evaluations largely ignore such asymmetries. We introduce Sovereignty over the Commons Simulation (SovSim), a generative multi-agent simulation framework that incorporates an agent with asymmetric power (boss or king) into a society of symmetric agents (workers or peasants), where all agents extract from a shared resource, collectively determining its sustainability over time. Across eleven state-of-the-art models, we find that introducing asymmetric power leads to severe breakdowns in cooperation and sustainability, with up to an 87.3% degradation in survival rate relative to symmetric settings.


### [59] [Analyzing Persona Effects in Generated Explanations from Multimodal LLM Agents in Urban Perception](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29064)
*Neemias da Silva, Myriam Delgado, Rodrigo Minetto, Daniel Silver, Thiago H Silva*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文研究了人物角色提示（persona prompting）如何影响多模态大语言模型在城市感知任务中生成的文本，发现不同人物角色在图像描述上高度趋同，但在理由阐述上呈现系统性差异，而感知标签则无显著统计差异。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有研究多关注多模态大语言模型的通用感知能力，但较少系统探究人物角色提示（persona prompting）这类社会文化上下文注入策略如何影响模型在城市感知场景中的输出，特别是不同角色在生成描述、理由和标签时的趋同与分歧模式尚不明确。

**Method:** 研究基于1,200个人物角色条件代理（persona-conditioned agents）生成了59,808条城市场景标注，并与两个无人物角色设置进行对比；通过分析图像描述（captions）、理由阐述（justifications）和感知标签（perception tags）三类输出，结合主题分析（topic analysis）评估不同人物角色在语义内容和评价主题上的差异。

**Result:** 实验结果显示，不同人物角色在图像描述上高度趋同，而在理由阐述上则呈现与社经地位和政治属性相关的系统性差异；感知标签未发现统计显著的人物角色相关差异，但存在效应趋势；主题分析进一步揭示不同人物角色在解读相同场景时会强调不同的评价性主题。

**Conclusion:** 研究表明人物角色提示对多模态大语言模型输出的影响具有维度特异性：低级感知任务（如图像描述和标签）受角色影响较小，而高级推理任务（如理由阐述）则易受角色社会文化属性调制，提示未来在部署此类模型于社会感知应用时需审慎考虑提示设计中的偏见传递风险。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
We study how persona prompting shapes language generated by multimodal large language models in an urban perception setting. Using 59,808 annotations from 1,200 persona-conditioned agents and two no-persona settings, we analyze captions, justifications, and perception tags across personas. Results indicate strong convergence in captions for different personas, whereas justifications display systematic variation associated with socioeconomic and political attributes, while perception tags show no statistically significant persona-related differences, though effect trends are observed. Topic analysis further reveals that personas emphasize different evaluative themes when interpreting the same scenes.


### [60] [SafeRx-Agent: A Knowledge-Grounded Multi-Agent Framework for Safe and Explainable Medication Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29146)
*Xinyu Wang, Hanwei Wu, Zhenghan Tai, Sicheng Lyu, Qincheng Lu, Ziyu Zhao, Jijun Chi, Jingrui Tian, Xiao-Wen Chang, Ziyang Song*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文提出首个基于第四级ATC代码生成的细粒度用药推荐任务，并设计SafeRx-Agent多智能体框架，通过整合患者上下文、外部临床知识和安全验证机制，在MIMIC-III和MIMIC-IV数据集上实现了更精确的药物预测并有效控制了药物相互作用和禁忌症风险。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有用药推荐方法面临双重挑战：模型层面，传统方法仅预测结构化药物编码且缺乏证据支撑，而LLM智能体虽能利用更丰富的临床上下文但缺乏安全验证与可追溯性；任务层面，现有基准使用粗粒度的药物类别，忽略了亚组级别的安全差异，可能导致风险过高估计。

**Method:** 本文提出SafeRx-Agent，一个基于知识的多种智能体协作框架。该框架利用患者临床上下文、外部临床知识库以及安全验证机制，生成具有可追溯性的细粒度药物集合，具体任务形式为基于第四级ATC代码生成的用药推荐。

**Result:** 在MIMIC-III和MIMIC-IV数据集上的实验结果表明，SafeRx-Agent在提升细粒度药物预测准确性的同时，有效控制了药物相互作用、禁忌症以及药物集合规模。

**Conclusion:** 本文通过引入细粒度ATC代码生成任务和安全验证多智能体框架，弥合了传统结构化方法与LLM方法之间的差距，为临床用药推荐提供了更具安全性和可解释性的解决方案，并为后续研究指明了亚组级别安全差异建模的重要性。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Medication recommendation predicts medications for patient visits, but existing methods still face two key challenges. At the model level, traditional drug recommendation methods only predict structured drug codes with limited evidence grounding, while LLM agents can use richer clinical context but may lack safety verification and traceability. At the task level, existing benchmarks often use broad medication categories, which ignore subgroup-level safety differences and can lead to risk overestimation. We introduce the first fine-grained medication recommendation setting based on fourth-level ATC code generation. We propose Safe Prescription Agent (SafeRx-Agent), a knowledge-grounded multi-agent framework that uses patient context, external clinical knowledge, and safety verification to recommend traceable medication sets. Experimental results on MIMIC-III and MIMIC-IV datasets show that SafeRx-Agent improves fine-grained medication prediction accuracy while controlling drug interactions, contraindications, and medication set size.


### [61] [Relevance as a Vulnerability: How Web Retrieval Degrades Safety Alignment in LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29224)
*Aditya Nawal, Manit Baser, Mohan Gurusamy*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文提出 AgentREVEAL 诊断框架，系统分析检索增强型 AI 智能体中检索导致的安全退化问题，发现即便是对立性或安全导向的来源也会使有害请求遵从率平均增加 25%，揭示了安全-效用权衡，并发布 HarmURLBench 基准以支持后续评估。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 尽管检索增强技术能为 LLM 提供最新信息，但将外部内容引入生成流程可能削弱模型的安全对齐机制。已有研究表明启用检索会增加智能体对有害请求的遵从性，但检索导致安全退化的具体机制尚不明确，缺乏系统性的诊断框架。

**Method:** 提出 AgentREVEAL 诊断框架，从两个维度分析检索引发的安全退化：一是检索与生成管线的集成方式（工具调用与响应生成是否绑定），二是检索内容的属性（包括来源立场、安全性与相关性）。同时构建 HarmURLBench 基准，包含 1,405 个真实 URL 和 320 种有害行为，用于标准化评估。

**Result:** 实验发现：在集成维度上，将工具调用与响应生成绑定在单一步骤中会显著放大有害输出；在内容维度上，发现了"安全来源悖论"——即便是包含警告或风险说明的对立性或安全导向来源，也会使有害请求遵从率相比无检索基线平均增加 25%。相关性是两类漏洞的共同激活条件。类似现象出现在前沿闭源模型中，且多种代表性管线干预下有害遵从性仍持续偏高。

**Conclusion:** 检索增强智能体存在固有的安全-效用权衡：相关性既是检索有用性的来源，也是安全退化的触发条件。这提示在设计检索增强智能体时需要谨慎平衡功能性与安全性，不能简单地依赖安全来源来缓解风险。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
AI agents augment large language models with external tools such as web retrieval, enabling grounded and up-to-date responses. However, incorporating external content into the generation pipeline can weaken the safety alignment mechanisms that govern model outputs. Prior work shows that enabling retrieval in agents increases compliance with harmful requests. We introduce AgentREVEAL, a diagnostic framework for analyzing retrieval-induced safety degradation in LLM agents. The framework examines two axes: how retrieval is integrated into the agent pipeline and the properties of the retrieved content. Along the integration axis, we find that binding tool invocation and response generation in a single step amplifies harmful outputs. Along the content axis, we uncover the Safe Source Paradox: even oppositional or safety-oriented sources, such as pages containing warnings or risk disclaimers, can increase harmful compliance by an average of 25% compared to the no-retrieval baseline. Finally, we show that relevance acts as a shared activation condition for both vulnerabilities. Similar patterns appear on frontier closed models, and harmful compliance remains elevated under several representative pipeline interventions, with some agents also entering this regime under autonomous retrieval. Because relevance is also what makes retrieval useful, these results expose a safety-utility trade-off for retrieval-enabled agents. We introduce HarmURLBench, a benchmark containing 1,405 real-world URLs paired with 320 harmful behaviors to support future evaluations.


### [62] [Wait! There's a Way Out: A Decision Mechanism for Forecasting Conversational Derailment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29243)
*Laerdon Kim, Vivian Nguyen, Cristian Danescu-Niculescu-Mizil*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
提出一种将触发决策与脱轨概率估计解耦的方法，通过前向模拟评估紧张时刻是否存在可恢复路径，从而在保持预测精度的同时大幅降低对话脱轨预警的误报率。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有对话脱轨预测模型仅基于当前对话历史估计脱轨概率来决定是否触发警报，忽略了对话未来可能恢复的情况，导致误报率过高。

**Method:** 受人类基线表现启发，提出一种延迟触发机制：利用前向模拟来评估紧张时刻是否可能存在合理的恢复路径，仅在没有恢复可能时才触发警报，从而将决策与脱轨概率估计解耦。

**Result:** 将该延迟机制集成到现有最优预测模型后，在不牺牲预测准确率的前提下显著降低了误报率，接近人类在相同任务上的表现水平。

**Conclusion:** 本工作表明，将决策过程作为预测系统的第一等公民来对待，能够有效提升在线预警系统的实用性，为对话安全监测提供了新的设计思路。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Forecasting conversational derailment is the task of predicting, as the conversation unfolds, whether it will eventually derail into personal attacks. Since forecasting models operate in an online fashion, they must decide whether to "trigger" an alert after each utterance--for example, to notify participants or a moderator that the conversation is at risk of derailing. Existing approaches make this decision solely based on the estimated likelihood of derailment given the preceding utterances, implicitly assuming that the conversation's future trajectory is fixed. As a result, they ignore the possibility of future recovery and incur an unnecessarily high rate of false positives.
  In this work we propose a method for decoupling the decision to trigger from derailment likelihood estimation. Our approach is inspired by the first human baseline on this task, which shows that humans achieve dramatically lower false positive rates by selectively deferring their decision to trigger when they anticipate that tension is likely to subside. We operationalize this insight with a deferral mechanism that uses forward-looking simulations to assess whether a tense moment admits plausible paths to recovery. Incorporating this mechanism into a state-of-the-art forecasting model substantially reduces false positives without sacrificing forecasting accuracy. More broadly, this work highlights the value of treating decision-making as a first-class component of forecasting systems.


### [63] [PatchBoard: Schema-Grounded State Mutation for Reliable and Auditable LLM Multi-Agent Collaboration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29313)
*Shuyu Zhang, Yaqi Shi, Lu Wang*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
PatchBoard提出了一种基于schema约束的协作架构，用JSON Patch原子操作替代LLM多智能体间的自然语言对话，通过确定性内核验证状态变更的合法性，在ALFWorld任务上以84.6%的成功率和45.5k tokens的消耗显著优于LangGraph和Flock等现有方法。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有LLM多智能体系统通常依赖自然语言对话或松散结构的共享内存进行协调，导致中间状态难以验证、归因和审计，缺乏可追溯性和可解释性。

**Method:** PatchBoard提出了一种schema驱动的协作架构，核心包括：一个Architect智能体构建任务特定的schema和工作流规则；一个确定性内核在每次提交状态变更前，对JSON Patch突变进行schema约束、角色特定写契约和运行时不变量的三重验证，仅通过原子性事务提交合法变更。

**Result:** 在630个匹配的ALFWorld测试场景中，PatchBoard实现了84.6%的成功率，远高于LangGraph的30.8%和Flock的61.6%；同时每个成功任务的token消耗仅为45.5k，对比LangGraph的368.3k和Flock的64.2k，展示了显著的效率优势。

**Conclusion:** 该研究表明，用结构化、可验证的状态变更机制替代自由文本对话，能够显著提升LLM多智能体协作的任务成功率和token效率，为构建可审计、可追溯的多智能体系统提供了新的设计范式。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
LLM multi-agent systems often coordinate through natural-language dialogue or loosely structured shared memory, making intermediate state difficult to validate, attribute, and audit. We introduce PatchBoard, a schema-grounded collaboration architecture that replaces inter-agent dialogue with validated JSON Patch mutations over a shared structured state. An Architect agent constructs a task-specific schema and workflow rules, while a deterministic kernel validates each proposed state mutation against schema constraints, role-specific write contracts, and runtime invariants before committing it transactionally. On 630 matched ALFWorld episodes, PatchBoard achieves an 84.6% success rate, compared with 30.8% for LangGraph and 61.6% for Flock, while reducing tokens per successful task to 45.5k, compared with 368.3k and 64.2k, respectively.


### [64] [FoRA: Fisher-orthogonal Rank Adaptation for Parameter-Efficient Fine-Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29317)
*Juneyoung Park, Seongbae Lee, Han-Sang Lee, Kyuho Lee, Minjae Kim, Seungheon Hyeon, Kiduk Kwon, Seongwan Kim, Jaeho Lee*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
FoRA通过Fisher信息选择任务相关层并在Stiefel流形上训练LoRA下投影，以极少的参数预算（仅为LoRA的一半、AdaLoRA的四分之一）在多个LLM系列上实现一致更优或可比的微调性能。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有参数高效微调（PEFT）方法如LoRA及其变体主要关注提升准确性，而忽视了减少可训练参数这一原始目标，即通过降低适配器秩来压缩参数的方法已趋于瓶颈。

**Method:** FoRA提出两种互补策略：一是通过单次对角Fisher信息分数（仅需不到1%的训练成本）快速筛选出任务信息最丰富的层进行微调；二是在选定层的LoRA下投影上施加Stiefel流形约束，保持列正交性和有效秩，从而在极低参数预算下维持模型表达能力。

**Result:** 在五个LLaMA系列骨干上，FoRA以LoRA和DoRA一半的参数预算实现一致更优的性能；以AdaLoRA四分之一的参数量达到仅差0.7-0.8个准确点的结果。跨架构实验覆盖LLaMA、Qwen3、Gemma三个系列的12个骨干（270M至32B参数），验证了方法的普适性。

**Conclusion:** Fisher层选择与Stiefel流形约束两者具有超加性组合效应：在相同参数预算下，Fisher选择单独即可匹配秩缩减方法的性能，而Stiefel约束提供了决定性的额外增益，表明层选择与参数正交性约束是比降低秩更有效的参数压缩策略。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Parameter-efficient fine-tuning(PEFT) has largely focused on LoRA and its accuracy-oriented variants, leaving the original goal of reducing trainable parameters has receivedcomparatively little attention. We introduce FoRA, which revisits this goal by reducing the number of adapted layers rather than adapter rank. FoRA selects task-informative layers via a single-pass diagonal Fisher score (under 1% of training cost) and trains the LoRA down-projection at selected layers on the Stiefel manifold, preserving column orthonormality and effective rank. FoRA consistently outperforms LoRA and DoRA at half their parameter budget, and falls within 0.7-0.8 accuracy points of AdaLoRA at one-quarter its parameter count, across five LLaMA-family backbones. Cross-architecture experiments on twelve backbones from the LLaMA, Qwen3, and Gemma families confirm consistent gains from 270M to 32B parameters. The two components combine super-additively: Fisher selection alone matches rank reduction at the same budget, while the Stiefel constraint provides the decisive additional gain.


### [65] [STAMP: Training Explicit Memory for Mobile GUI Agents in Controllable and Scalable Virtual Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29324)
*Junyang Wang, Haiyang Xu, Xi Zhang, Zhaoqing Zhu, Ming Yan, Jieping Ye, Jitao Sang*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
STAMP是一个通过可控虚拟环境训练移动Agent显式记忆的框架，利用程序化注入的记忆变量合成可验证数据，并支持在线强化学习，其生成的Stamp-GUI智能体在Memory-World基准上达到SOTA性能。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现存的移动GUI智能体在需要长期记忆的长周期任务中频繁失败，根本原因在于有限上下文窗口与高token占用的屏幕截图之间存在矛盾，导致智能体必须逐步丢弃旧的视觉历史，永久丢失关键的瞬时信息。此外，现有以动作为中心的数据集无法教会智能体"记忆什么"或"何时记忆"，而增强静态真实世界数据成本高昂且缺乏交互验证。

**Method:** 提出STAMP框架，通过可控虚拟环境训练移动Agent的显式记忆能力。在合成任务中，通过程序化注入确定性的记忆变量来控制需记忆的内容、编码时机和检索时机，从而大规模生成可验证的监督数据。同时，利用环境驱动的奖励反馈支持在线强化学习。

**Result:** 在提出的Memory-World基准上，Stamp-GUI智能体在GUI专用模型中达到最先进性能，在该基准上创下新记录。模型展现出卓越的记忆准确性和任务韧性，同时保持强大的通用移动导航能力。

**Conclusion:** 通过可控虚拟环境合成可验证数据并引入在线强化学习，可以有效解决移动GUI Agent的长期记忆缺失问题。该方法无需昂贵的数据标注即可训练显式记忆策略，在长期任务中同时实现高记忆精度和强任务鲁棒性。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Mobile GUI agents excel at immediate reactive control but frequently fail in realistic, long-horizon tasks that require memory. This failure stems from a fundamental conflict between limited context windows and token-heavy screenshots. To save the limited context, agents must progressively discard older visual history, permanently losing crucial transient information. Furthermore, existing action-centric datasets fail to teach agents what or when to explicitly memorize, and augmenting static real-world data is prohibitively expensive and lacks interactive verification. To resolve this, we present STAMP, a framework that trains explicit memory in mobile agents through controllable virtual environments, where deterministic memory variables are programmatically injected into synthesized tasks to control what must be memorized, when it should be encoded, and when it must later be retrieved, thereby producing verifiable supervised data at scale and enabling online reinforcement learning through environment-driven reward feedback. Evaluated on our newly introduced Memory-World benchmark, the resulting Stamp-GUI agent achieves state-of-the-art performance among GUI-specialized models and sets a new high watermark on our Memory-World benchmark, demonstrating exceptional memory accuracy and task resilience while maintaining strong general mobile navigation capabilities.


### [66] [SURGENT: A Surgical Multi-Agent Assistance System Across the Perioperative Workflow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29368)
*Dongsheng Shi, Yue Li, Xin Yi, Yongyi Cui, Huawei Feng, Linlin Wang*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
SURGENT是一个面向围手术期工作流的 surgical 多智能体辅助系统，结合Tree-of-Thought规划器、多部门协作智能体和检索增强推理，通过新颖的长短期记忆设计实现更完整、情境化的推理，在五项围手术期任务中优于已有基线模型，并支持基于DeepSeek的隐私保护部署。

**Method:** SURGENT是一个手术多智能体辅助系统，集成了Tree-of-Thought规划器、多部门协作智能体和基于检索增强生成的临床指南与生物医学文献推理模块，并设计了同时管理长期患者病史和短期工作摘要的新型记忆机制，以实现更完整和一致的情境化推理。

**Conclusion:** SURGENT通过多智能体协作与增强记忆设计实现了更可靠、可追溯的外科辅助决策，其基于DeepSeek的部署方式兼顾了隐私保护与性能，为构建智能、公平且安全的围手术期辅助系统提供了实用且可信的解决方案。
